< Text>
I frequently buy gas here - low prices and no debit card fee. I had my car smog checked and it was great. The tech was polite, friendly, and CLEAN! He handled the equipment with gloves and my car with soft towels. Really, it was unbelievable.
The online coupon has a $20 discount, and that's what I was charged (plus the smog certificate $8 fee). I've used coupons at other places and they always had an excuse why the vehicle wasn't eligible for the reduced rate.
I highly recommend Berkeley Smog & Gas for a STAR station test that's quick and pleasant.< /Text>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< Text>
I live in Arizona but was in town and needed a cut so decided to give Salon Bordeaux a try. The area is super cute (Starbucks across the street and antique shops down the way) and the salon is adorable. Very cool and hip yet comfortable. I especially liked the retro/vintage hair dryers, posters, etc. on display!

I had my hair cut with Jess who was amazing. I have had the same hair cut/style forever and she made some really good suggestions and let me decide what I wanted to do. She's super talented at what she does.

I also made an appointment for a facial and waxing which they were able to get me in at the last minute.  The products were top notch (Phytomer from France) and the esthetician couldn't have been nicer. Yes, you can hear a bit what is going on outside but it wasn't distracting in any way.

Plan to arrive a bit early to find parking. It's a cool, busy area so it's not surprising that it's sometimes hard to find a spot! A great place to buy someone a gift certificate to get pampered. I will definitely be coming back each time I'm in town! Thank you!</Text>

1566233400802< /Time>
< rating>
4<//rating>
< review>
Among the best taco shop food. Ingredients and  prep are excellent, the portions more than generous, and a really good salsa bar.  2 of us split a 12 rolled tacos, which was not only a huge meal for $4.50 each, but was also good crispy tacos, and more guac and cheese than I think I've ever seen on an order like this.  Good guac too.

Better than average decor and seating.  The hand painted murals are fun and quirky, and the seating, tho nothing special, is clean and comfortable.  They have both booths and tables with chairs, and seating for 30-40 I'd guess.

The average reviewer would give them a 5. I don't unless I can't think of anything not perfect, or there's something over the top amazing.  Everything is good to excellent, but nothing over the top amazing, and there's 2 minor things missing.  There's no drive thru, which makes sense given the physical setup if the building, but a taco shop just isn't complete without a drive thru, and there's no labels on the salsa bar.  (And thinking about it, I'd like a milder red salsa available too)

The only other note is that I don't know if there's a public restroom.  There's nothing visible in the restaurant, but there's other sections of the building that may have something available.  If there's nothing here, the casino and mini Mart at Funner (Rincon) is 3 minutes away, but unless you're going to the casino at Funner (or Pauma, or Pala, or La Jolla, or Valley View) eat at Jilbertos.< /review>

The actual dental work was quite good.  Both Doctors who worked on me were thoughtful, kind and experienced.  This office desperately need lessons in organization.  During my initial visit it was determined I would need medical release from my nephrologist before my molar could be extracted.  I provided them with his fax number and was told the extraction would be scheduled upon his release.  The office called the following Friday saying the release was in and I was given an appt date and time.  Upon arrival I was placed in a room where I sat for nearly an hour before someone came in to tell me that the release had indeed not been given.  After 40 minutes I was informed I was good to go on the procedure but that I had to take 4 antibiotics and wait an hour before they could begin.  Actual removal of my broken molar began around 12:30 and continued until 4 pm, at which time I was told that I would have to go to their oral surgeon in Eastvale.  An appt was made for 8 am on the 17th of June. I arranged for a ride only to receive a call at 7:45 telling me the surgeon was ill and all appts for that day were cancelled.  A new appt was scheduled for 6/29 with the oral surgeon.  As I had a huge hole in my mouth I contacted the dental office to see if an earlier appt could be arranged.  I was contacted on Wed the 24th that I could get the root removed by another dentist at 11 am that day.  On the way to this appt. As I initially said, the doctors were very good and pleasant, but this was an ordeal from hell.  People underestimate the value of organization and accuracy. She misdiagnosed which tooth was causing pain, she missed the HUGE abscess that was under the tooth, and she WAYYYYYYYY under prescribed the proper dose of antibiotics for the infection.
